msg:The name of the Midnight Hotel is taken from Mao Dun's novel "Midnight". It is opposite the parking lot of Dongzha Scenic Area and very close to Dongzha Scenic Area. It is not far from Xizha Scenic Area. Belongs to Wuzhen official hotel.
On the table in the room there was a note of welcome from the general manager, as well as complimentary cakes and alcohol wipes. The bathroom and shower room are separated, which is different from most hotels. I like it very much. The room decoration is also unique, and there are also Mao Dun's books. When I checked in, I bought a coupon for 150 yuan for the east-west gate, and I swiped my face when I took the photo. In the evening, after having dinner nearby, we walked to the Xizha Scenic Area for a walk and just swiped our faces to enter. There is also a hotel shuttle bus at the entrance of the scenic spot, just use the red receipt given when you check in at the hotel. After visiting the night view in the evening, I entered again the next day and directly scanned my face. The Jiangnan water town and cultural journey are completely in line with this Wuzhen cultural tourism experience.

msg:Traveling to Wuzhen this spring, we stayed at the Midnight Hotel (the name of the hotel is obviously taken from the novel "Midnight" by the writer Mao Dun, because Mao Dun is from Wuzhen). We stayed for 2 nights and had a great experience. First, the hotel is in a good location. Opposite is the Dongzha Scenic Area, which is only a step away. When going to Xizha, the hotel has a free shuttle bus that departs every half hour, which is very convenient. The hotel also provides free sightseeing buses in the scenic area.
Second, the hotel caters well. It offers a set meal of only 168 yuan, with 6 dishes, which is enough for a family of four, and it is very delicious, especially the salt-baked white water fish, special sauce-flavored duck and sister-in-lawâ€™s tofu. My friend After eating it, I was full of praise. Breakfast is buffet style and very rich. Compared with those who spend 300 to 500 yuan per person on meals at scenic spots, this hotel can be called a conscientious enterprise.
Third, many details are admirable.
â€”â€”Red serving chopsticks. We are accustomed to using serving chopsticks when dining out. Although most hotels provide them, they are of the same color, so it is easy to get confused when eating. The serving chopsticks in Midnight Hotel are red, so there is no mistake.
â€”â€”A toilet seat in the bathroom. For guests who are a bit mysophobic or particularly particular, this move must be appreciated.
â€”â€”Books in the guest room. For book lovers, the books displayed in the room are like meeting old friends in a foreign country. Although there are not many books, they have a common theme, which is to introduce all aspects of Wuzhen so that you can have an in-depth understanding of Wuzhen's history and culture through the scenery when traveling.
â€”â€”The TV has a playback function. The hotels we stayed in ranged from luxurious to simple, and there were quite a lot of them. The TVs rarely played back the TV sets. During the trip, I often felt regretful that I couldn't watch my favorite programs. It was really surprising to find that the TV set in the Midnight Hotel could make up for this regret!
Fourth, the hotel has a good service attitude.
Special thanks to the waiters Ms. Liu and Manager Zhou for their considerate service.
I wonâ€™t introduce details like this one by one. I strongly recommend tourists to experience it by themselves. We will choose Midnight again when we come to Wuzhen.
